CREATE TABLE fingerprints (fingerprint_id INT PRIMARY KEY, user_id INT REFERENCES users(user_id), fingerprint_data BYTEA, timestamp TIMESTAMPTZ)</t><s>REVOKE SELECT, INSERT, UPDATE, DELETE ON iris_scans FROM user_role</s>
